Citrus fragrance for women and men. <b>Afternoon Swim </b> was launched in 2019. The nose behind this fragrance is Jacques Cavallier Belletrud. </p><div v-pre class='fragrantica-blockquote'><p>Les Colognes Louis Vuitton is the new line of the Les Parfums Louis Vuitton collection that comes out in April 2019. Perfumer Jacques Cavallier Belletrud signed all creations of this house. The three fresh, cologne-like scents (in EDP concentration) are named Sun Song, Cactus Garden and Afternoon Swim.</p>

<p>Louis Vuitton collaborated with L.A.-based artist Alex Israel, who designed the outer packaging of the new fragrances. The flacons and boxes come in a bright yellow, green and blue, with drawings of a sun, a cactus and a wave.</p>

<p>Afternoon Swim is a "full of energy" scent, with orange, bergamot and mandarin. "I wanted a shot of vitamin C in the fragrance, something full of energy," explained Cavallier Belletrud.</p>

<p>The fragrances will be available as a 100 and 200 ml Eau de Parfum.</p></div><p class="reviewstrigger" style="font-size: smaller; color: #83a6c4">Read about this perfume in other languages: <a     <div class="strike-title"><span>All Reviews By Date</span></div>
    <div class="grid-x grid-padding-x grid-margin-y" style="position: relative; padding: 0 0.25rem 0 0.25rem;">
        <div class="cell destinationreview"></div>                    <div id="parent2338072" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(248,249,236,0.87);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:3,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:1,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:2,&quot;sillage&quot;:1,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;male_unisex&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;had&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="3"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc2338072" class="cell small-2" ><div ><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="Verdure80"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1685620"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/avatari/m.1685620.jpg" class="comments-avatar"alt="Verdure80" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"><span class="idLinkify" title="/perfume/Creed/Spice-and-Wood-10101.html"><img loading="lazy" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/perfume/mm.10101.jpg"class="perfume-wearing-icon" alt="Spice and Wood"title="Spice and Wood"></span></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma2338072ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck0x3"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd2338072" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"><div class="flex-child-shrink" style="background: rgba(248,249,236,0.87); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1685620">Verdure80</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-11-04"></span><fromunixtime unixtime="1730761443" class="vote-button-legend"></fromunixtime></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>Completely unremarkable. The opening is pleasant, like you just peeled a mandarin orange. After the 30 minute perceivable life of the scent, it dries down to a bitter, sour skin scent. Sold my bottle after coming to terms with this as a Louis Vuitton fanboy. Disappointing!</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="53947"comment_id="2338072"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Louis-Vuitton/Afternoon-Swim-53947.html?ccid=2338072#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2337315" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(248,249,236,0.8);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:4,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:1,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;female_unisex&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="4"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; I love the simplicity of it, and I frankly don't understand why people complain about longevity when it's a straight up citrus fragrance.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="53947"comment_id="2336506"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Louis-Vuitton/Afternoon-Swim-53947.html?ccid=2336506#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2335906" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,245,242,0.86);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:4,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:1,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;had&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="4"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc2335906" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="Sniffing Jin"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/2292211"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/avatari/m.2292211.jpg" class="comments-avatar"alt="Sniffing Jin" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"><span class="idLinkify" title="/perfume/Yves-Saint-Laurent/Babycat-73149.html"><img loading="lazy" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/perfume/mm.73149.jpg"class="perfume-wearing-icon" alt="Babycat"title="Babycat"></span></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma2335906ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck0x3"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd2335906" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(250,245,242,0.86); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/2292211">Sniffing Jin</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-11-02">11/02/24 13:55</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>Man does this smell good, but MAN is the performance abysmal.<br />
<br />
Super uplifting citrus with orange being the star player.  Amazing inoffensive freshie great for all warm weather occasions.  But... I really tried to figure out if the performance was trash or if I was going nose blind. Spoiler: the performance is trash.  <br />
<br />
TEST ONE: Sprayed on skin, projection was actually super strong, but I noticed it was gone within an hour, MAYBE two.  Sprayed again the next day and at the hour and half mark asked multiple people if they smelt anything on me, in which they said something along the lines of "Kind of, but barely".<br />
<br />
TEST TWO:  Sprayed on clothes, found it lasted a little bit longer maybe 3-4 hours total. Better responses from others around me as well, but still weak.  Next day sprayed on a t-shirt and just left it in my room got similar results around 3-4 hours.  <br />
<br />
All in all, Pretty loud projection actually, but wont get past that 3-4 hour ceiling. Don't be afraid to overspray and feel free to hit your clothes if needed.  Smells amazing but I cannot justify the poor performance for this price point.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="53947"comment_id="2335906"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Louis-Vuitton/Afternoon-Swim-53947.html?ccid=2335906#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2335252" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(247,244,242,0.85);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:1,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:4,&quot;sillage&quot;:3,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;unisex&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc2335252" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="TheDogfatherHTX"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1824841"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/avatari/m.1824841.jpg" class="comments-avatar"alt="TheDogfatherHTX" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"><span class="idLinkify" title="/perfume/Louis-Vuitton/Imagination-67370.html"><img loading="lazy" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/perfume/mm.67370.jpg"class="perfume-wearing-icon" alt="Imagination"title="Imagination"></span></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma2335252ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck0x3"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd2335252" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(247,244,242,0.85); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1824841">TheDogfatherHTX</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-11-02">11/02/24 00:51</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>Onto my second Louis Vuitton fragrance review; Afternoon Swim. This one is on par with Imagination for the amount of hype it receives. I've seen at least a few "Top X Louis Vuitton" lists on YouTube, and Afternoon Swim is usually near the top. I remember smelling this at the LV boutique, but I don't necessarily remember being impressed. However, I figured if that many people say it's a gem then maybe I missed something. With that in mind, I picked up a sample to give it a proper review. Let's get into it;<br />
<br />
Scent:<br />
The opening is citrusy and fresh spicy. The notes listed are orange, bergamot, ambergris, and ginger; and I can pick up on all of them. The most prominent notes are the orange and bergamot. Similar to Meteore, the orange notes are photo-realistic; juicy and tart with a bit of sweetness thrown in. The bergamot adds more citrus while adding a bit of spiciness. This is followed by the ginger and ambergris. The ginger adds more fresh spiciness while the ambergris rounds out the opening with a subtle, oceanic warmth. The dry down is pretty much the same as the opening, with the primary difference being that the ambergris is stronger. That warm, salty, oceanic accord gets boosted and helps to balance out the citrus in the dry down.<br />
<br />
Performance:<br />
Initial projection is surprisingly strong and fills the room. Sillage is strong as well with an easily noticeable scent trail. After a few hours the projection was still strong at around 6 feet, and the scent trail was still easily noticeable. At about the 8 hour mark the projection was still about 3-4 feet and the scent trail had faded but was still noticeable. At hour 10 the fragrance was still barely hanging on. The projection was within arms length and the scent trail was faint, but it was still there. The fragrance wore off and became a skin scent before hour 12, but still really solid performance for something so citrus-forward.<br />
<br />
When to wear:<br />
This is a spring/summer scent most suitable for daytime wear. I could see myself wearing this during the day running around town, or at the pool/on the beach. This is a very casual fragrance, so I wouldn't pick it to wear on a date, to the office, or anything formal.<br />
<br />
Blind buy:<br />
If you like citrus bombs this is a safe blind buy for you.<br />
<br />
Final verdict:<br />
So it looks like Afternoon Swim turned out to be worthy of the hype after all. The scent was much better on my skin than it was on a test strip, the performance was spectacular for such a fresh fragrance, and the scent itself was a hit with everyone that caught a whiff of it. Now like I said with Meteore, I find it hard to see myself paying $330 for a bottle of this. But I'm absolutely going to keep my eyes open for a decent clone of this, and if (big if) I ever see LV's hit discounters this will be one I try to grab. But hey, if you have the money and you want a killer warm weather scent, you can't go wrong with Afternoon Swim.<br />
<br />
Scent: 9/10<br />
Longevity: 8/10<br />
Sillage: 8/10</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="53947"comment_id="2335252"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Louis-Vuitton/Afternoon-Swim-53947.html?ccid=2335252#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,249,251,0.9); align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="53947"comment_id="2326951"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Louis-Vuitton/Afternoon-Swim-53947.html?ccid=2326951#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2323000" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(255,253,234,0.81);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc2323000" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="dudegetsmoney"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/2071768"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/avatari/m.2071768.jpg" class="comments-avatar"alt="dudegetsmoney" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"><span class="idLinkify" title="/perfume/Louis-Vuitton/Pacific-Chill-81423.html"><img loading="lazy" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/perfume/mm.81423.jpg"class="perfume-wearing-icon" alt="Pacific Chill"title="Pacific Chill"></span></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma2323000ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck0x3"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd2323000" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(255,253,234,0.81); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/2071768">dudegetsmoney</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-10-21">10/21/24 13:04</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>Afternoon Dive (by Montagne) vs. Afternoon Swim:<br />
<br />
Afternoon Dive is a direct clone by Montagne. Now I'm not a big fan of clones, but I've read a lot of good shit about Montagne, so I decided to try it out.<br />
<br />
TLDR: They are very similar.<br />
<br />
AD is a great clone. Capturing the simplicity of the ginger and citrus combo, along with the ambergris in the background. In fact, if I let you smell AD without a side by side comparison, 99% of noses won't be able to distinguish that it's not actually AS. Now this is a $45 (50ml) fragrance. Let's keep that in mind whilst I talk about the differences.<br />
<br />
The major difference I think for AD is that it's less citrusy. It's slightly harsher, less sweet, and more jagged than Afternoon Swim. It also has more musk, and just a hint of woodiness in the back. AD also smells different on clothes. It's noticeably more synthetic. AS is much more smooth, with sweetish citrus. Yes, AS smells better, that's no doubt. Both on clothes and on skin, I much prefer AS. Now performance, AD is stronger, and performs better than Afternoon Swim. We all know that AS isn't the best in performance. <br />
<br />
So, if you're not a big fragrance fanatic, and don't want to drop $300-$500 on AS, then AD is a no-brainer blind buy, as long as you take what the differences I say into consideration. You're saving about 3x more on AD compared to AS (new bottle), and about 2x on a refill. <br />
<br />
Me personally, I'm still going for AS. Afternoon Swim is simply incredible, and I must have it in my collection. <br />
9/10 clone. Completely blind buyable if you like Afternoon Swim.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="53947"comment_id="2323000"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Louis-Vuitton/Afternoon-Swim-53947.html?ccid=2323000#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2319406" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(255,253,234,0.84);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:1,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:2,&quot;sillage&quot;:2,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;unisex&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; My. Mandarine. Afternoon Swim by Louis Vuitton is not just a summer fragrance—it's an intergalactic olfactory cataclysm that grabs your senses, tosses them into the sun, and leaves you floating in a pool of pure citrus ecstasy.<br />
<br />
You think you know what "fresh" smells like? You don't. Not until you've been drenched in the juice of a thousand perfectly peeled mandarines, each note more zesty and electrifying than the last. The opening is an explosion of citrus so crisp, it's like a bright orange comet tearing through your synapses, leaving behind a trail of pure sunshine.<br />
<br />
And don’t get me started on the notes! The sparkling mandarin orange absolutely dances with bergamot and Sicilian lemon, creating a cocktail that feels like Poseidon himself handed you a citrus-infused lightning bolt to wear on your skin.<br />
<br />
9.5/10 because even the gods of fragrance need some room for improvement.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="53947"comment_id="2297528"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Louis-Vuitton/Afternoon-Swim-53947.html?ccid=2297528#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2295853" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(247,244,242,0.87);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:0,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; <br />
🍊🫚🌊 Afternoon swim by @louisvuitton is probably the most amazing fresh perfume ever made. It opens up with the brightest, most beautiful, juicy mandarin and orange combination and then it dries down into an aquatic sea salt form of ambergris. It is a photorealistic citrus perfume without it smelling like a cleaner whatsoever. Afternoon swim sparkles with a hit of that aquatic ambergris. Unfortunately it does not last so long. It is also my favorite layering perfume with all of my perfumes. If i want to brighten a perfume and add some citruses, I layer it with afternoon swim. 🌊🫚🍊</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="53947"comment_id="2295853"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Louis-Vuitton/Afternoon-Swim-53947.html?ccid=2295853#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2292595" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(255,253,234,0.75);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:0,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1517239">Wafflepuffs</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-09-15">09/15/24 03:51</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>The name "Afternoon Swim" perfectly describes what this fragrance is.<br />
The swim is refreshing and invigorating, yet it's in the afternoon so it's soothing and relaxing, maybe even a bit playful.<br />
The opening and dry-down perfectly reflect this, burst of a sweet citrus orange in the opening, and clean and soothing in the dry-down.<br />
Between Afternoon Swim and Pacific Chill, I think both are great and it's up to preference which is better—you can't go wrong. Pacific Chill is citrus and fruits all throughout even until the dry-down, extremely juicy and tropical.<br />
However, you can go wrong. The longevity and sillage are just terrible for what you're paying for and are extremely disappointing for how good the scents are.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; It smells like a rich man on a yacht off the French Riviera or off the Campania Amalfi coast eating a fancy &amp; expensive dinner in the middle of July. I really love the smell, but I was devastated by the lackluster performance. It only lasts about 2-3 hrs on me and for what LV charges that’s completely inexcusable. Jacques should’ve added ambroxan in this and it would easily be the #1 fresh LV fragrance.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="53947"comment_id="2283053"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Louis-Vuitton/Afternoon-Swim-53947.html?ccid=2283053#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2276665" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,249,251,0.78);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:0,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; This one is in my top 5 of all time rn. My most used and favourite summer/spring freshie. Smells simple but high quality, which I appreciate.<br />

padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc2211688" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="ōyiss"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1592869"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/avatari/m.1592869.jpg" class="comments-avatar"alt="ōyiss" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma2211688ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck1x2"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd2211688" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(250,245,242,0.76); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1592869">ōyiss</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-07-08">07/08/24 05:50</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>Feels like summer-bottled. <br />
<br />
Fruity citruses, sweet amber, airy yet watery. Smells tropical and blue. It should be illegal to work whilst smelling like this; Afternoon Swim begs to be worn outside under a blue sky while the wearer is having a good time. This is a perfect summer holiday scent. <br />
<br />
Due to the sweetness in this fragrance, Afternoon Swim really teeters on the line of young &amp; fun - but I don’t really see this being out of place worn by anyone. It’s a good feeling, it’s a happy vibe - happiness has no limits.<br />
<br />
All of this said, is it for me?… no, unfortunately it’s not (at least, not all of the time). <br />
<br />
I really like this fragrance but I’ve kind of gone off of sweet fragrances for the moment. I actually prefer smelling this on my wife more than I enjoy being in a scent bubble of this all day. My affinity of Afternoon Swim comes and goes like waves; in fact much like the ocean waves that this reminds me of!</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="53947"comment_id="2211688"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Louis-Vuitton/Afternoon-Swim-53947.html?ccid=2211688#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2209484" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(254,252,238,0.7);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:4,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:1,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:3,&quot;sillage&quot;:2,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;male_unisex&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="4"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc2209484" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="Chrononomicon"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1262147"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/avatari/m.1262147.jpg" class="comments-avatar"alt="Chrononomicon" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma2209484ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck0x3"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd2209484" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(254,252,238,0.7); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1262147">Chrononomicon</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-07-05">07/05/24 18:07</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>Straightforward citrus scent but definitely mouthwatering and photorealistic. <br />
<br />
Some faint aquatic notes and ambroxan float in the background. As it dries down it becomes more notably synthetic due to the lack of natural fixatives. <br />
<br />
The entire approach to the composition of this fragrance is very similar to Kerosene's Summer of 84, except Summer of 84 has a sharper and more synthetic grapefruit note at the top. The mandarin orange here in Afternoon Swim is very convincing but that's all the fragrance will give you.<br />
<br />
Weirdly enough, if you smell too close to the skin as it dries down you can get a whiff of corn tortilla chips/corn tostadas. Xerjoff's Kobe and Mefisto (Both 2009) have a similar note and it seems to be tied to whatever citrus aromachemicals they're using - just an interesting tidbit.<br />
<br />
Ultimately, it's hard to dislike this fragrance, especially in the sillage, but is it worth the price? F**** NO. <br />
<br />
The same people who are saying this type of extortion is justified are the same people who'd mistake 'Afternoon Swim' for you rubbing your neck with a fresh Clementine from Whole Foods.<br />
<br />
And in this economy? Not a bad idea, honestly. Both scents would last the same amount of time, anyway.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="53947"comment_id="2209484"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Louis-Vuitton/Afternoon-Swim-53947.html?ccid=2209484#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2209242" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,245,242,0.9);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:1,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:3,&quot;sillage&quot;:2,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;male_unisex&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1992810">RifleZz</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-06-15">06/15/24 10:49</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>I 100% agree with the person's post that is a few posts belove mine. This scent has no base. It is this lively combination of citruses and aquatic notes that I LOVE. Once I applied it on my skin, I could not smell it at all, but a few seconds after it started to come to life. Picture the best cold and refreshig Fanta that is natural and polished. As I was going in for a second sniff, I could not smell the citruses, but I smelled the aquatic notes and the amberis. Those to me smell like you are by the pool and you are about to jump in, I like this part of the fragrance as well. But as I distance my nose from my hand, I start to smell those awsome and natural citruses. This fragrance is moving, and it is reminding me of the sea - the scent starts off and there is no smell, but then the citruses come up, then they calm down and the ambergris and aquatic notes come up, and so on. It is a cycle which I'm in love with.<br />
The performance is average, 2 hours of good projection and sillage (after that, it becomes a skin scent which lasts around 7 hours).<br />
I highly suggest that you try this scent on your own skin and then make the decision of buying this expensive scent. It is worth it for me because I enjoy those citruses so damn much!<br />
One of the best, if not the best summer scent of all time for me!<br />
10 / 10!</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="53947"comment_id="2189173"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Louis-Vuitton/Afternoon-Swim-53947.html?ccid=2189173#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2186733" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(249,249,243,0.78);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:1,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="1"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; Because it has a simple profile it relies on the quality of the ingredients to get the message across. Feels like a luxury fragrance for sure. You know exactly what you are smelling and there’s no hidden agenda or drastic changes in the dry down, it just gets softer and less sharp, more musky as time passes. Simply re-apply if you want the top notes again. I must admit it is quite addictive to me. It’s calming and relaxing but fresh and energising at the same time. It has a certain meditative quality to it. <br />
Very much unisex, not especially “masculine” <br />
Might suit younger people more…as a  42yr old man, I sort of feel like I’m at the very limit of being able to pull this off, but I like it so much I’d happily wear it for myself and not worry about what anyone else thinks.<br />
Good for beach/seaside. Lasts a long time on clothing and projects well.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="53947"comment_id="2179116"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Louis-Vuitton/Afternoon-Swim-53947.html?ccid=2179116#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2176402" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(247,244,242,0.73);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:0,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:1,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:4,&quot;sillage&quot;:1,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;unisex&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; And yes. For me it was impulsive purchase (like JustasL mentioned) when I just happened to walk by the local Louis Vuitton boutique.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="53947"comment_id="2156636"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Louis-Vuitton/Afternoon-Swim-53947.html?ccid=2156636#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2155849" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(255,253,234,0.73);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:3,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:1,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="3"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc2155849" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="JustasL"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1591936"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/avatari/m.1591936.jpg" class="comments-avatar"alt="JustasL" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"><span class="idLinkify" title="/perfume/Roja-Dove/Enigma-Pour-Homme-20559.html"><img loading="lazy" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/perfume/mm.20559.jpg"class="perfume-wearing-icon" alt="Enigma Pour Homme"title="Enigma Pour Homme"></span></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma2155849ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck2x1"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd2155849" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(255,253,234,0.73); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1591936">JustasL</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-05-14">05/14/24 12:27</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>Louis Vuitton's "Afternoon Swim" plunges you into a synthetic citrus realm, overwhelmed by the pervasive presence of ambroxan—it's essentially an ambroxan bomb. Noticeably absent is any genuine ambergris, leaving the scent devoid of any natural depth. Rather than offering photo-realistic citruses, it mimics the candied zest of orange-flavored soft drinks like Fanta, failing to deliver a true-to-life citrus experience.<br />
<br />
Indeed, “Afternoon Swim” ranks as one of the more overhyped entries in the world of luxury perfumery. Its simplicity might attract the general public, yet it fails to impress those with a more discerning olfactory palette. For a fragrance carrying Louis Vuitton’s hefty price tag, one might expect a more intricate or daring composition. Sadly, it delivers little beyond a pleasant yet mundane experience. This fragrance appears to be best suited for those whose ventures into luxury are as impulsive as their purchases—more a souvenir than a signature scent.<br />
<br />
Overall, “Afternoon Swim” is underwhelming and overpriced, failing to justify its cost with any remarkable olfactory aspects.<br />
<br />
Rating: 6/10 — pleasant scent, yet disappointingly ordinary for the discerning enthusiast.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="53947"comment_id="2155849"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Louis-Vuitton/Afternoon-Swim-53947.html?ccid=2155849#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2153463" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(254,252,238,0.72);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:0,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; Absolute perfection. Only hitch is that the performance is disappointing for such a beautiful scent, however I have noticed many state that it gets better after a few months &amp; to be honest, that could be possible as my Virgin Island Water is strangely very strong after time! If this frag had a scent trail &amp; performance of the likes of Ganymede for example, this would probably be amongst the top echelon of compliment getters. Anyone who finds the scent of this one anything short of stunning, may need their nose tested! Also, smells absolutely nothing like Tygar, which is also an awesome fragrance. I will get a bottle of this &amp; hope the performance amps up over time but for now, will overspray (when I get it). padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc2094978" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="MrBolton"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1161847"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/avatari/m.1161847.jpg" class="comments-avatar"alt="MrBolton" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"><span class="idLinkify" title="/perfume/Creed/Original-Vetiver-468.html"><img loading="lazy" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/perfume/mm.468.jpg"class="perfume-wearing-icon" alt="Original Vetiver"title="Original Vetiver"></span></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma2094978ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck5x1"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd2094978" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(249,249,243,0.84); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1161847">MrBolton</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-03-16">03/16/24 23:01</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>I bought Afternoon Swim in Maui last Summer. All items from LV are discounted in Hawaii due to the import tax laws there, so it's the only way you'll get it less than retail. I think it was 6% off and their sales tax is only 4.16%. Just FYI as a perk of being in paradise.<br />
This is the most mouthwatering citrus out there. My wife aptly remarked it smells like orange Fanta soda; she ain't too wrong and loves this one on me. Gorgeous orange peels (like an orange soda), salty ambergris, and smooth ambroxan are what I get. This is one of the few fragrances I own that I get occasional compliments on, and I've got a lot of heavy hitters in my collection.<br />
<br />
Many complain about performance. Honestly, when I first got my bottle after using up my samples that I had for a while, I felt very letdown. I read people on here all the time being drama queens saying how they can't smell something after a few hours, and that never happens to me. Something may become a close skin scent, but it's basically never that I literally can smell nothing in 4-5 hours, maybe less--which is what happened at first for me.<br />
Had it been reformulated? Did it get spoiled in shipping? I emailed LV, and they were precisely no help at all, saying, "Sorry, sucker!" But in a more polite way. I regretted buying this, wishing I opted for Pacific Chill whose sample was giving me amazing performance.<br />
Well, the secret for Afternoon Swim is maceration, which is a good sign of LV using natural ingredients. After about 4-6 months, my bottle has COME ALIVE. Completely different wearing experience. This thing is an absolute beast mode citrus performer for massive sillage and longevity. Super potent juice. I can spray it in the morning, work in the office all day, go sweat on a bike ride, shower, and then I can still smell decently strong hints of it on my wrist--10+ hours later. I have very few fragrances of this genre that can touch what this pulls off.<br />
So, haters, don't be so quick to dismiss this--especially if you like the opening. Just wear it for a few months and let the maceration process begin. You'll come back to a new and much improved animal in not much time at all. For those wanting the best fragrance for Summer, you better buy your bottle ASAP!<br />
<br />
THAT ASIDE, this vs Tygar shouldn't even be a debate. Tygar is one of the most overhyped fragrances out there, or at least I think so after wearing it as an Afternoon Swim owner and lover. Tygar is black and white, while Afternoon Swim is vibrant HD color. They're definitely cousins, but it's clear whom the more successful one is. <br />
I wear this year round, but it's best in warm weather. On a cold winter day indoors, it's nice to bring a ray of sunshine in, and that's exactly what this does.<br />
Easily a 10/10 for me. If I had to reduce my collection from 125+ down to 5 or less, this would be in there. Heck, if I had to go to 2, it's probably going to be this and something else. 16 years into fragrances, 6 years into niche, and Afternoon Swim is a clear standout. I will never be without a bottle in the collection. I should've never waited to buy this!<br />
Blind buy safe if you're into fresh marine citrus scents. Again, maceration will make a world of difference.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="53947"comment_id="2094978"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Louis-Vuitton/Afternoon-Swim-53947.html?ccid=2094978#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2094427" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(247,244,242,0.81);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:4,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:1,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;had&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="4"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; <br />

<br />
This is completely unisex and a really pleasing fragrance to wear on a hot summer day; projection and performance could improve but I think it’s fair enough.<br />

I feel bad for those who wasted money on this and didn’t like it, hopefully you sampled first. I mean, this isn’t supposed to be a beast mode clubbing perfume in the first place, I think it’s has more like a BLISS AQUATIC vibe. Kinda of like the watery vibe from Cactus but a million times better and nicer smelling with a touch of citrus sweetness. Also reminiscent to Météore but more aquatic and citrus instead of soft fruit like Météore has. Tranquil, gender neutral unisex. I love that I get this MANDARIN, ICE POPS, AND BLUE RASPBERRY JELLO scent (even though raspberry isn’t listed) IN THE BEST WAY POSSIBLE. It’s hard to put in perspective because it can be for summer but also nice in winter, ironically, so it’s season neautral also. See it as a cool man/woman aquatic that’s lingers close to the skin.<br />
<br />
I sampled it before purchasing it and it grew on my BF and I, we have the huge 6.8 bottle now, half way done and can’t wait to refill it.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; I tested this today so its worth noting it is a 30 degrees F winter day.  <br />
<br />
For me, the scent doesnt seem to be anything too special.  It does smell good. Its clean, blue, and I get a lot of mandarin.  The scent is pretty linear for me as it seems to stay consistent the same from opening all the way to the end.  But again, its a nice scent and you can tell it is a quality frag.  But nothing ground breaking. <br />
<br />
For the price, I definitely wont pick up a FB.  But I do want a LV frag at some point.  With their refill policy I think the price IS high but not as absurd as some people make it seem.  <br />
Will try imagination or l'mmensite soon.  <br />
<br />
For Afternoon Swim,<br />
Scent - 8/10<br />
Projection - 7/10<br />
Longevity - 8/10<br />
Price - 5/10<br />
<br />
Overall will give it a 7.5</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="53947"comment_id="2001739"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Louis-Vuitton/Afternoon-Swim-53947.html?ccid=2001739#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2001126" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(247,244,242,0.79);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:0,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; Ah... Hum. Hmm. Yeah, I'm disappointed.<br />
<br />
I couldn't test any of them against my skin at the time but smelling them from the bottle this one stood out to me most and it smelled HEAVENLY - both in the bottle and on my skin I smell a hidden lime note. There's also that familiar masculine musk I detect in almost all male fragrances (and many marketed as unisex, such as this one)... I definitely feel there's more to Afternoon Swim than just "bergamot" and "orange". The longevity also far surpasses my expectations - much like many Jo Malones, I expected it to stick around for only 30 minutes to 1 hour, but here we are 3 hours in and I can still smell it, albeit very faintly... honestly that's really good for a purely citrus fragrance with no substantial base notes.<br />
<br />
Now to explain where my disappointment lays: the other reviews are correct, this really is like 'sunshine in a bottle'. But you know what it reminded me of? Sun by Lush, which you can get for £20/30ml or £40/100ml... versus Afternoon Swim which is £255/100ml... sooooo I guess I'm buying a bottle of Sun lol</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1750980">jillvee</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2023-09-07">09/07/23 12:06</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>Due to the longevity and very minimal projection of this scent i'd have to rate it as just ok, due to the retail price. That being said, it is a more sophisticated citrus with depth. Upon first spray I actually get the headier notes of bitter bergamot/tea and the peel/pith of citrus that quickly develops into the mandarin. Although not listed, on me it has a bit of a pomelo/grapefruit vibe that transforms into a more blue aquatic skin scent at drydown (almost reminds me of the 90s davidoff cool water woman or acqua di gioia but just a tiny hint). This is a quick metamorphosis and one that needs more sprays and more application. But if you are looking for a good layering scent, one that wears close to the skin and may be perfect for office/teachers and those who are more sensitive to overpowering scent, I could see this as a great pick-me-up in cooler months to beat the Winter blues but is a great uplifting scent overall, just needs reapplication.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/906635">NickZee</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2023-04-27">04/27/23 15:08</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>Note pyramid is incomplete, in addition to orange citruses I get ginger, tea, ambroxan and a touch of white florals.  Doesn’t have any of the usual aquatic notes one might expect - no calone, chlorinated water, salty water or seaweed here.  The opening is huge and dwarfs the drydown which is why I think it is accused of poor performance, but in reality it is perceptible for many hours.    Just dont expect that orange blast to last, it transitions into the ginger to give an impression of continuity.  Lasts a lot better on outer layers of clothes (18 hours+ on jackets) than it does on skin, though I find performance acceptable on skin (5-6 hours from 10 sprays).  In the deep drydown it smells similar to LV’s own L’immensite as the ginger and ambroxan seem to be the last notes standing.  Overall an excellent fragrance that can be dressed up or down.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="53947"comment_id="1819308"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Louis-Vuitton/Afternoon-Swim-53947.html?ccid=1819308#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent1649069" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,245,242,0.87);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:1,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; - The minimalist combination of aldehydes, citrus oils/accords and woody ambers really invokes the titular feeling of an afternoon swim: sun rays, fresh cool water and chlorine in a swimming pool. <br />
